    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport json\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 1) Locate the active workspace directory\ndirs = [d for d in os.listdir(\'.\') if d.startswith(\'workspace\') and os.path.isdir(d)]\nif not dirs:\n    print("‚ùå No workspace directory found. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the printable Wikipedia page for Survivor\ntitle = "Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nurl = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title={title}&printable=yes"\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n}\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor printable page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\nresp.raise_for_status()\nprint(f"Page fetched successfully (status {resp.status_code})\\n")\n\n# 3) Parse HTML with BeautifulSoup\ndoc = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Find the simple winners-only table (headers exactly [\'Season\',\'Winner\']), then fallback\ntables = doc.find_all(\'table\', class_=\'wikitable\')\ntarget = None\nprint(f"Found {len(tables)} wikitable(s). Looking for simple winners-only table...\\n")\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(tables, 1):\n    first = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    if not first:\n        continue\n    hdrs = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)]\n    if hdrs == [\'season\', \'winner\']:\n        target = tbl\n        print(f"‚Üí Selected simple winners-only table #{idx} with headers {hdrs}\\n")\n        break\n# fallback: any table containing both \'season\' & \'winner\'\nif not target:\n    print("Simple table not found ‚Äì falling back to any table containing \'Season\' & \'Winner\'...\\n")\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(tables, 1):\n        first = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first:\n            continue\n        hdrs = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)]\n        if \'season\' in hdrs and \'winner\' in hdrs:\n            target = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Selected fallback table #{idx} with headers {hdrs}\\n")\n            break\nif not target:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find any suitable table with Season & Winner. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 5) Determine the column indices for Season and Winner\nfirst = target.find(\'tr\')\ncolumns = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in first.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)]\nseason_idx = columns.index(\'season\')\nwinner_idx = columns.index(\'winner\')\nprint(f"Column indices -> season: {season_idx}, winner: {winner_idx}\\n")\n\n# 6) Extract season‚Üíwinner pairs\nwinners = []\nfor row in target.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:  # skip header row\n    cells = row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    if len(cells) <= max(season_idx, winner_idx):\n        continue\n    s_txt = cells[season_idx].get_text(strip=True)\n    if not s_txt.isdigit():\n        continue\n    season_num = int(s_txt)\n    if not (1 <= season_num <= 44):\n        continue\n    # prefer <a> tag text, else plain text\n    winner_cell = cells[winner_idx]\n    a = winner_cell.find(\'a\')\n    if a and re.search(r\'[A-Za-z]\', a.get_text()):\n        name = a.get_text(strip=True)\n    else:\n        name = winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season_num} ‚Üí Winner: \'{name}\'")\n    winners.append({\'season\': season_num, \'winner\': name})\n\n# 7) Sort and validate\nwinners_sorted = sorted(winners, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nprint(f"\\nTotal winners extracted: {len(winners_sorted)} (expected 44)")\nif len(winners_sorted) != 44:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: extracted count != 44. Please verify the logic and page structure.")\n\n# 8) Write to JSON\noutput_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(output_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(winners_sorted, f, indent=2)\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Saved winners list to: {output_path}")',

Please verify logic and page structure.")\nelse:\n    missing = [w[\'season\'] for w in winners_sorted if not w[\'winner\']]\n    if missing:\n        print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è Seasons with empty winners: {missing}")\n\n# 8) Write to JSON\nout_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(out_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(winners_sorted, f, indent=2)\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Winners list saved to: {out_path}")\n',

Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the standard (non-printable) Wikipedia page for Survivor\ntitle = "Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nurl = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/{title}"\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n}\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers=headers)\nresp.raise_for_status()\nprint(f"Page fetched successfully (status {resp.status_code})\\n")\n\n# 3) Parse HTML with BeautifulSoup\ndoc = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) First, scan ALL <table> tags for a simple 2-column winners-only table [\'Season\',\'Winner\']\nprint("Scanning all tables for a simple 2-column Season‚ÜíWinner table...\\n")\ntarget = None\nall_tables = doc.find_all(\'table\')\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(all_tables, 1):\n    first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    if not first_row:\n        continue\n    hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\', \'td\'], recursive=False)\n    hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n    # debug print of header row lengths\n    print(f"Table {idx} headers: {hdr_texts}")\n    if hdr_texts == [\'season\', \'winner\']:\n        target = tbl\n        print(f"‚Üí Selected simple 2-column winners-only table #{idx}. Headers match exactly [\'Season\',\'Winner\']\\n")\n        break\n\n# 5) Fallback: if no simple table, scan only wikitable-class tables for any containing both keywords\nif not target:\n    print("No exact 2-column table found; falling back to any .wikitable containing Season & Winner...\\n")\n    wikitables = doc.find_all(\'table\', class_=lambda v: v and \'wikitable\' in v)\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, 1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\', \'td\'], recursive=False)\n        hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n        if \'season\' in hdr_texts and \'winner\' in hdr_texts:\n            target = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Fallback selected wikitable #{idx} with headers containing Season & Winner: {hdr_texts}\\n")\n            break\n\nif not target:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find any suitable table with Season & Winner. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 6) Determine column indices for Season and Winner\ndef extract_header_indices(tbl):\n    first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\', \'td\'], recursive=False)\n    texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n    return texts.index(\'season\'), texts.index(\'winner\')\n\nseason_idx, winner_idx = extract_header_indices(target)\nprint(f"Column indices -> season: {season_idx}, winner: {winner_idx}\\n")\n\n# 7) Extract Season‚ÜíWinner entries\nwinners = []\nfor row in target.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:  # skip header row\n    cells = row.find_all([\'th\', \'td\'], recursive=False)\n    # ensure enough cells\n    if len(cells) <= max(season_idx, winner_idx):\n        continue\n\n    # parse season number\n    season_text = cells[season_idx].get_text(strip=True)\n    if not season_text.isdigit():\n        continue\n    season_num = int(season_text)\n    if season_num < 1 or season_num > 44:\n        continue\n\n    # extract winner name: prefer <a> link text\n    winner_cell = cells[winner_idx]\n    a_tag = winner_cell.find(\'a\')\n    if a_tag and re.search(r\'[A-Za-z]\', a_tag.get_text()):\n        name = a_tag.get_text(strip=True)\n    else:\n        name = winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season_num} ‚Üí Winner: \'{name}\'")\n    winners.append({\'season\': season_num, \'winner\': name})\n\n# 8) Sort & verify count\nwinners_sorted = sorted(winners, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nprint(f"\\nTotal winners extracted: {len(winners_sorted)} (expected 44)")\nif len(winners_sorted) != 44:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: Extracted count != 44. Verify table structure or page updates.")\nelse:\n    # flag any empty winners\n    missing = [w[\'season\'] for w in winners_sorted if not w[\'winner\']]\n    if missing:\n        print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è Seasons with missing winner names: {missing}")\n\n# 9) Save to JSON\nout_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(out_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(winners_sorted, f, indent=2)\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Winners list saved to: {out_file}")",\n  ',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport re\nimport json\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 1) Locate the active workspace directory\ndirs = [d for d in os.listdir(\'.\') if d.startswith(\'workspace\') and os.path.isdir(d)]\nif not dirs:\n    print("‚ùå No workspace directory found. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\npage_title = "Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nurl = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/{page_title}"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\nresp.raise_for_status()\nprint(f"Page fetched successfully (status {resp.status_code})\\n")\n\n# 3) Parse HTML\ndoc = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Try selecting the two-column "Winners" table via section\nprint("Attempting to locate the \'Winners\' section table...\\n")\ntarget = None\nspan = doc.find(\'span\', id=\'Winners\')\nif span:\n    h2 = span.find_parent(\'h2\')\n    if h2:\n        for sib in h2.next_siblings:\n            if sib.name == \'table\':\n                # check header row\n                first_row = sib.find(\'tr\')\n                if not first_row:\n                    continue\n                hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n                hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n                print(f"Found table after \'Winners\' heading with headers: {hdr_texts}")\n                # check exact two-column table\n                if len(hdr_texts) == 2 and hdr_texts[0] == \'season\' and hdr_texts[1] == \'winner\':\n                    target = sib\n                    print("‚Üí Selected the 2-column Winners table from section.\\n")\n                else:\n                    print("‚Üí Table did not match 2-column format, continuing search")\n            # break once we passed the first table if found\n            if target:\n                break\n\n# 5) Fallback: scan all tables for a 2-col header exactly [\'Season\',\'Winner\']\nif not target:\n    print("Fallback: scanning all <table> tags for exact 2-column [\'Season\',\'Winner\']...\\n")\n    all_tables = doc.find_all(\'table\')\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(all_tables, 1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n        hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n        if len(hdr_texts) == 2 and hdr_texts[0] == \'season\' and hdr_texts[1] == \'winner\':\n            target = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Selected 2-column table #{idx} in fallback with headers: {hdr_texts}\\n")\n            break\n\n# 6) Second fallback: scan all .wikitable for headers containing both \'season\' & \'winner\'\nif not target:\n    print("Second fallback: scanning .wikitable tables for headers containing both \'season\' & \'winner\'...\\n")\n    wikitables = doc.find_all(\'table\', class_=lambda v: v and \'wikitable\' in v)\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, 1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n        hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n        print(f"Wikitable #{idx} headers: {hdr_texts}")\n        if \'season\' in hdr_texts and \'winner\' in hdr_texts:\n            target = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Selected wikitable #{idx} with headers containing Season & Winner.\\n")\n            break\n\nif not target:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find any suitable winners table. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 7) Determine column indices for Season and Winner\ndef get_header_indices(tbl):\n    first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n    season_i = texts.index(\'season\')\n    winner_i = texts.index(\'winner\')\n    return season_i, winner_i\n\nseason_idx, winner_idx = get_header_indices(target)\nprint(f"Column indices -> season: {season_idx}, winner: {winner_idx}\\n")\n\n# 8) Extract season‚Üíwinner pairs\nwinners = []\nfor row in target.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:  # skip header row\n    cells = row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    if len(cells) <= max(season_idx, winner_idx):\n        continue\n    # parse season number\n    season_text = cells[season_idx].get_text(strip=True)\n    m = re.match(r"^(\\d+)", season_text)\n    if not m:\n        continue\n    season = int(m.group(1))\n    if not (1 <= season <= 44):\n        continue\n    # extract winner name(s)\n    winner_cell = cells[winner_idx]\n    a_tags = winner_cell.find_all(\'a\')\n    if a_tags:\n        names = [a.get_text(strip=True) for a in a_tags if re.search(r"[A-Za-z]", a.get_text())]\n        name = \' & \'.join(names) if names else winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    else:\n        name = winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season} ‚Üí Winner: \'{name}\'")\n    winners.append({\'season\': season, \'winner\': name})\n\n# 9) Sort and verify\nwinners_sorted = sorted(winners, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nprint(f"\\nTotal winners extracted: {len(winners_sorted)} (expected 44)")\nif len(winners_sorted) != 44:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: Extracted count != 44. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\npage_title = "Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nurl = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/{page_title}"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\nresp.raise_for_status()\nprint(f"Page fetched successfully (status {resp.status_code})\\n")\n\n# 3) Parse the HTML\ntxt = resp.text\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(txt, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) FIRST PASS: scan every <table> for an exact two-column header [\'Season\',\'Winner\']\nprint("Scanning all <table> tags for exact 2-column [Season, Winner] header...\\n")\ntables = soup.find_all(\'table\')\nprint(f"Total tables found: {len(tables)}")\ntarget = None\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(tables, 1):\n    first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    if not first_row:\n        continue\n    hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n    if len(hdr_texts) == 2:\n        print(f"  Table #{idx} header: {hdr_texts}")\n        if hdr_texts == [\'season\', \'winner\']:\n            target = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Selected table #{idx} as the exact two-column Winners table.\\n")\n            break\n\n# 5) SECOND PASS: fallback to any .wikitable containing both \'season\' & \'winner\'\nif not target:\n    print("No exact 2-column table found. Falling back to scanning .wikitable tables...\\n")\n    wikitables = soup.find_all(\'table\', class_=lambda v: v and \'wikitable\' in v)\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, 1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        hdr_cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n        hdr_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in hdr_cells]\n        print(f"  Wikitable #{idx} header: {hdr_texts}")\n        # ensure both keywords present\n        if \'season\' in hdr_texts and \'winner\' in hdr_texts:\n            target = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Selected wikitable #{idx} containing Season & Winner.\\n")\n            break\n\n# 6) Abort if still not found\ndef bail():\n    print("‚ùå Could not find a suitable winners table. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nif not target:\n    bail()\n\n# 7) Determine indices for Season and Winner columns\ndef get_header_indices(tbl):\n    first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    cells = first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    texts = [c.get_text(strip=True).lower() for c in cells]\n    return texts.index(\'season\'), texts.index(\'winner\')\n\nseason_i, winner_i = get_header_indices(target)\nprint(f"Column indices -> season: {season_i}, winner: {winner_i}\\n")\n\n# 8) Extract season->winner pairs\nwinners = []\nfor row in target.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:  # skip header row\n    cells = row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    if len(cells) <= max(season_i, winner_i):\n        continue\n    # parse season number\n    s_txt = cells[season_i].get_text(strip=True)\n    m = re.match(r"^(\\d+)", s_txt)\n    if not m:\n        continue\n    season = int(m.group(1))\n    if not (1 <= season <= 44):\n        continue\n    # extract winner name(s)\n    w_cell = cells[winner_i]\n    links = w_cell.find_all(\'a\')\n    if links:\n        names = [a.get_text(strip=True) for a in links if re.search(r"[A-Za-z]", a.get_text())]\n        name = \' & \'.join(names) if names else w_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    else:\n        name = w_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season} ‚Üí Winner: \'{name}\'")\n    winners.append({\'season\': season, \'winner\': name})\n\n# 9) Sort and verify count\nwinners_sorted = sorted(winners, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nprint(f"\\nTotal winners extracted: {len(winners_sorted)} (expected 44)")\nif len(winners_sorted) != 44:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: Extracted count != 44. Verify table selection and page structure.")\nelse:\n    print("‚úÖ Correct number of winners found.")\n\n# 10) Save to JSON\nout_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(out_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(winners_sorted, f, indent=2)\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Winners list saved to: {out_path}")',

Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\npage_title = "Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nurl = f"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/{page_title}"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresponse = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\nresponse.raise_for_status()\nprint(f"Page fetched successfully (status {response.status_code})\\n")\n\n# 3) Parse the HTML with BeautifulSoup\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Attempt to find the exact two-column Winners table under the "Winners" heading\nprint("Locating the two-column winners table under the \'Winners\' section...\\n")\nspan_winners = soup.find(\'span\', id=\'Winners\')\ntarget_table = None\n\nif span_winners:\n    # The <span id="Winners"> is inside the <h2>; we find its parent then look for the next table sibling\n    h2 = span_winners.find_parent(\'h2\')\n    if h2:\n        for sib in h2.find_next_siblings():\n            if sib.name == \'table\':\n                # Inspect header row\n                first_tr = sib.find(\'tr\')\n                if first_tr:\n                    headers = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first_tr.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)]\n                    print(f"  Found table after \'Winners\' heading with headers: {headers}")\n                    if headers == [\'season\', \'winner\']:\n                        target_table = sib\n                        print("‚Üí Selected this table as the two-column winners list.\\n")\n                        break\n        if not target_table:\n            print("  Table after \'Winners\' heading did not match exactly [\'Season\',\'Winner\']. Falling back.\\n")\nelse:\n    print("No \'Winners\' section found. Falling back to scanning all tables.\\n")\n\n# 5) If still not found, scan every <table> tag for exact 2-column header match\nif not target_table:\n    print("Scanning ALL <table> tags for an exact two-column [\'Season\',\'Winner\'] header...\\n")\n    all_tables = soup.find_all(\'table\')\n    print(f"Total tables on page: {len(all_tables)}")\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(all_tables, start=1):\n        first_tr = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_tr:\n            continue\n        hdr_texts = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first_tr.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)]\n        if len(hdr_texts) == 2:\n            print(f"  Table #{idx} header: {hdr_texts}")\n            if hdr_texts == [\'season\', \'winner\']:\n                target_table = tbl\n                print(f"‚Üí Selected table #{idx} as the exact two-column winners table.\\n")\n                break\n    if not target_table:\n        print("No exact two-column table found in full scan. Falling back to .wikitable search.\\n")\n\n# 6) Final fallback: scan .wikitable tables containing both \'season\' & \'winner\'\nif not target_table:\n    print("Fallback: scanning .wikitable tables for headers containing \'season\' & \'winner\'...\\n")\n    wiki_tables = soup.find_all(\'table\', class_=lambda c: c and \'wikitable\' in c)\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wiki_tables, start=1):\n        first_tr = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_tr:\n            continue\n        hdr_texts = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first_tr.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)]\n        print(f"  Wikitable #{idx} header: {hdr_texts}")\n        if \'season\' in hdr_texts and \'winner\' in hdr_texts:\n            target_table = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Selected wikitable #{idx} containing Season & Winner.\\n")\n            break\n\n# 7) Abort if no appropriate table is found\ndef bail():\n    print("‚ùå Could not find a suitable winners table. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nif not target_table:\n    bail()\n\n# 8) Determine the indices of the Season and Winner columns dynamically\ndef get_header_indices(table):\n    first_tr = table.find(\'tr\')\n    cells = first_tr.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    texts = [cell.get_text(strip=True).lower() for cell in cells]\n    return texts.index(\'season\'), texts.index(\'winner\')\n\nseason_idx, winner_idx = get_header_indices(target_table)\nprint(f"Identified column indices -> season: {season_idx}, winner: {winner_idx}\\n")\n\n# 9) Extract season‚Üíwinner pairs for seasons 1 through 44\nwinners = []\nfor tr in target_table.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:  # skip header row\n    cells = tr.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    if len(cells) <= max(season_idx, winner_idx):\n        continue\n    # Parse season number\n    season_text = cells[season_idx].get_text(strip=True)\n    m = re.match(r"^(\\d+)", season_text)\n    if not m:\n        continue\n    season_num = int(m.group(1))\n    if not (1 <= season_num <= 44):\n        continue\n    # Extract winner name(s)\n    winner_cell = cells[winner_idx]\n    link_tags = winner_cell.find_all(\'a\')\n    if link_tags:\n        names = [a.get_text(strip=True) for a in link_tags if a.get_text(strip=True)]\n        winner_name = \' & \'.join(names) if names else winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    else:\n        winner_name = winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season_num} ‚Üí Winner: \'{winner_name}\'")\n    winners.append({\'season\': season_num, \'winner\': winner_name})\n\n# 10) Sort by season and verify count\nwinners_sorted = sorted(winners, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nprint(f"\\nTotal winners extracted: {len(winners_sorted)} (expected 44)")\nif len(winners_sorted) != 44:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: Extracted count != 44. Please verify table selection and page structure.")\nelse:\n    print("‚úÖ Correct number of winners found.\\n")\n\n# 11) Save the results to JSON\noutput_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(output_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(winners_sorted, f, indent=2)\nprint(f"‚úÖ Winners list saved to: {output_path}")',

Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\nurl = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching page: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\nresp.raise_for_status()\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 3) Find the <span id="Winners"> heading and select the first <table> after it\nprint("Locating the Winners table under the \'Winners\' section...\\n")\nspan_winners = soup.find(\'span\', id=\'Winners\')\nif not span_winners:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find a <span id=\'Winners\'> element. Page structure may have changed.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n# Find its heading tag (likely <h2>)\nheading = span_winners.find_parent([\'h2\',\'h3\',\'h4\'])\nif not heading:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find the parent heading for the Winners section.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n# Iterate siblings until we hit a table\ntarget_table = None\nfor sib in heading.find_next_siblings():\n    if sib.name in [\'h2\',\'h3\',\'h4\']:\n        # Reached next section without finding table\n        break\n    if sib.name == \'table\':\n        target_table = sib\n        print("‚Üí Found table immediately after the \'Winners\' heading.\\n")\n        break\nif not target_table:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find a table immediately after the \'Winners\' heading.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 4) Verify the header row contains exactly two <th> cells: Season and Winner\nheader_tr = target_table.find(\'tr\')\nif not header_tr:\n    print("‚ùå Winners table has no header row.\\n")\n    sys.exit(1)\nth_cells = header_tr.find_all(\'th\', recursive=False)\nheaders = [th.get_text(strip=True) for th in th_cells]\nprint(f"Detected header cells: {headers}\\n")\nif [h.lower() for h in headers] != [\'season\',\'winner\']:\n    print("‚ùå Table header does not match [\'Season\',\'Winner\']. Found: {headers}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 5) Extract Season‚ÜíWinner pairs for seasons 1 through 44\nwinners = []\nfor row in target_table.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:  # skip header row\n    cells = row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'], recursive=False)\n    if len(cells) < 2:\n        continue\n    # Season number\n    season_txt = cells[0].get_text(strip=True)\n    m = re.match(r"^(\\d+)", season_txt)\n    if not m:\n        continue\n    season = int(m.group(1))\n    if not (1 <= season <= 44):\n        continue\n    # Winner name\n    winner_cell = cells[1]\n    links = winner_cell.find_all(\'a\')\n    if links:\n        names = [a.get_text(strip=True) for a in links if re.search(r"[A-Za-z]", a.get_text())]\n        winner_name = \' & \'.join(names) if names else winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    else:\n        winner_name = winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season} ‚Üí Winner: \'{winner_name}\'")\n    winners.append({\'season\': season, \'winner\': winner_name})\n\n# 6) Sort and verify count\nwinners_sorted = sorted(winners, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nprint(f"\\nTotal winners extracted: {len(winners_sorted)} (expected 44)")\nif len(winners_sorted) != 44:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: Extracted count != 44. Verify the Winners table structure.")\n\n# 7) Save to workspace/survivor_winners_list.json\noutput_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(output_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(winners_sorted, f, indent=2)\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Winners list saved to: {output_path}")',

    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 1) Locate the active workspace directory\ndirs = [d for d in os.listdir(\'.\') if d.startswith(\'workspace\') and os.path.isdir(d)]\nif not dirs:\n    print("‚ùå No workspace directory found. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\nurl = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page for debug generation...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Error fetching page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 3) Generate debug info: for each H2/H3/H4 heading with a .mw-headline span, record id/text and number of tables until next header\ndebug_lines = []\nfor header_tag in soup.find_all([\'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\']):\n    span = header_tag.find(\'span\', class_=\'mw-headline\')\n    if not span or not span.get(\'id\'):\n        continue\n    hid = span.get(\'id\')\n    text = span.get_text(strip=True)\n    # Count <table> siblings under this section until next header\n    tbl_count = 0\n    for sib in header_tag.find_next_siblings():\n        if sib.name in [\'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\']:\n            break\n        if sib.name == \'table\':\n            tbl_count += 1\n    debug_lines.append(f"{header_tag.name} id=\'{hid}\' text=\'{text}\' ‚Üí {tbl_count} table(s)")\n\n# 4) Write debug info to file\ndbg_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_debug_headings.txt\')\nwith open(dbg_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write("# Debug: H2/H3/H4 headings and number of tables until next heading\\n")\n    for line in debug_lines:\n        f.write(line + "\\n")\n\n# 5) Output for tester\nprint(f"‚úÖ Debug info generated: {dbg_path}")\nprint("=== Contents ===")\nfor line in debug_lines:\n    print(line)\nprint("=== End of debug info ===")',

Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page for debug generation\nurl = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page for debug generation...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Error fetching page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 3) Parse HTML and collect all section headings\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\ndebug_lines = []\n\n# For each <span class="mw-headline">, record its id, text, parent heading tag, and number of tables until next heading\nfor span in soup.select(\'span.mw-headline\'):\n    hid = span.get(\'id\', \'\')\n    text = span.get_text(strip=True)\n    parent = span.find_parent([\'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\'])\n    parent_tag = parent.name if parent else \'UNKNOWN\'\n    # Count tables until the next heading of same/higher level\n    tbl_count = 0\n    if parent:\n        for sib in parent.find_next_siblings():\n            if sib.name in [\'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\']:\n                break\n            if sib.name == \'table\':\n                tbl_count += 1\n    debug_lines.append(f"{parent_tag} id=\'{hid}\' text=\'{text}\' ‚Üí {tbl_count} table(s)")\n\n# 4) Write debug info to file\ndbg_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_debug_headings.txt\')\nwith open(dbg_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write("# Debug: section headings and count of tables until next heading\\n")\n    for line in debug_lines:\n        f.write(line + "\\n")\n\n# 5) Print summary for tester\ngood = len(debug_lines) > 0\nprint(f"‚úÖ Generated debug info: {dbg_path}")\nprint("=== Contents of survivor_debug_headings.txt ===")\nfor line in debug_lines:\n    print(line)\nprint("=== End of debug info ===")\nif not good:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: No headings were captured.     "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 1) Locate the active workspace directory\ndirs = [d for d in os.listdir(\'.\') if d.startswith(\'workspace\') and os.path.isdir(d)]\nif not dirs:\n    print("‚ùå No workspace directory found. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\nwiki_url = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {wiki_url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(wiki_url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64)\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    print(f"‚Üí HTTP {resp.status_code} OK")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Failed to fetch page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 3) Parse HTML\ntxt = resp.text\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(txt, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Collect debug info for each section heading (h2/h3/h4 .mw-headline)\ndebug_lines = []\nspans = soup.find_all(\'span\', class_=\'mw-headline\')\nprint(f"Found {len(spans)} section headlines (.mw-headline spans)\\n")\nfor span in spans:\n    hid = span.get(\'id\', \'\')\n    text = span.get_text(strip=True)\n    parent_heading = span.find_parent([\'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\'])\n    parent_tag = parent_heading.name if parent_heading else \'UNKNOWN\'\n    # count tables until the next heading of same or higher level\n    tbl_count = 0\n    if parent_heading:\n        for sib in parent_heading.find_next_siblings():\n            if sib.name in [\'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\']:\n                break\n            if sib.name == \'table\':\n                tbl_count += 1\n    debug_line = f"{parent_tag} id=\'{hid}\' text=\'{text}\' ‚Üí {tbl_count} table(s)"\n    debug_lines.append(debug_line)\n\n# 5) Write debug info to survivor_debug_headings.txt\ndbg_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_debug_headings.txt\')\nwith open(dbg_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    f.write("# Debug: section headings (h2/h3/h4) with .mw-headline and count of tables until next heading\\n")\n    for line in debug_lines:\n        f.write(line + "\\n")\n\n# 6) Print debug info\nprint(f"‚úÖ Debug info written to: {dbg_file}\\n")\nprint("=== Contents of survivor_debug_headings.txt ===")\nfor line in debug_lines:\n    print(line)\nprint("=== End of debug info ===")\n\n# 7) Sanity check\nif not debug_lines:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: No headings captured. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\nwiki_url = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {wiki_url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(wiki_url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64)\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    print(f"‚Üí HTTP {resp.status_code} OK\\n")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Failed to fetch page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 3) Parse HTML and find the correct winners table\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\ntables = soup.find_all(\'table\')\nprint(f"Found {len(tables)} tables on the page. Searching for the winners table...\\n")\n\nwinner_table = None\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(tables, start=1):\n    # Get header cells\n    header = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n    if not header:\n        continue\n    cols = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in header.find_all([\'th\', \'td\'])]\n    # Look for \'season\' and \'winner\' in first two columns\n    if len(cols) >= 2 and \'season\' in cols[0] and \'winner\' in cols[1]:\n        winner_table = tbl\n        print(f"‚Üí Matched winners table at index {idx} (header: {cols[:3]})\\n")\n        break\n\nif not winner_table:\n    print("‚ùå Could not locate the winners table. The page structure may have changed.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 4) Parse rows: extract seasons 1‚Äì44 and winners\ndata = []\nrows = winner_table.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]  # skip header\nfor row in rows:\n    cells = row.find_all([\'td\', \'th\'])\n    if len(cells) < 2:\n        continue\n    # Season number\n    season_text = cells[0].get_text(strip=True).split()[0]  # take first token\n    try:\n        season_num = int(season_text)\n    except:\n        continue\n    if season_num > 44:\n        continue\n    # Winner name\n    winner_cell = cells[1]\n    # Use link text if available, else full text\n    link = winner_cell.find(\'a\')\n    winner_name = link.get_text(strip=True) if link else winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    data.append({\n        \'season\': season_num,\n        \'winner\': winner_name\n    })\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season_num}: {winner_name}")\n\nif not data:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è No winners data parsed. Check table parsing logic.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 5) Save to JSON\nout_path = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(out_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(data, f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)\n\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Successfully wrote {len(data)} entries to: {out_path}")',

    "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport json\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 1) Locate the active workspace directory\ndirs = [d for d in os.listdir(\'.\') if d.startswith(\'workspace\') and os.path.isdir(d)]\nif not dirs:\n    print("‚ùå No workspace directory found. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\ndata_url = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {data_url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(data_url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    print(f"‚Üí HTTP Status: {resp.status_code} OK\\n")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Failed to fetch page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 3) Parse HTML\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Find the "Series overview" table by caption\nwikitables = soup.find_all(\'table\', class_=\'wikitable\')\nprint(f"Found {len(wikitables)} wikitables on the page. Scanning for \'Series overview\' caption...\\n")\nseries_table = None\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, start=1):\n    cap = tbl.find(\'caption\')\n    cap_text = cap.get_text(strip=True).lower() if cap else \'\'\n    print(f"Table {idx}: caption=\'{cap_text}\'")\n    if \'series overview\' in cap_text:\n        series_table = tbl\n        print(f"‚Üí Matched \'Series overview\' table at index {idx}\\n")\n        break\n\n# 5) Fallback: match header row containing both \'Season\' and \'Winner\'\nif not series_table:\n    print("No caption match found, trying header‚Äêbased fallback...\\n")\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, start=1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        headers = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'])]\n        print(f"Fallback check Table {idx}: headers={headers[:5]}")\n        if \'season\' in headers and \'winner\' in headers:\n            series_table = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Fallback matched table at index {idx}\\n")\n            break\n\nif not series_table:\n    print("‚ùå Could not locate the Series overview table. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 6) Identify column indices for Season and Winner\nheader_cells = series_table.find(\'tr\').find_all([\'th\',\'td\'])\ncol_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True) for c in header_cells]\nprint(f"Series overview columns: {col_texts}\\n")\ncol_lower = [t.lower() for t in col_texts]\ntry:\n    season_idx = col_lower.index(\'season\')\n    winner_idx = col_lower.index(\'winner\')\nexcept ValueError:\n    # try partial matches\n    season_idx = next((i for i,t in enumerate(col_lower) if \'season\' in t), None)\n    winner_idx = next((i for i,t in enumerate(col_lower) if \'winner\' in t), None)\n\nif season_idx is None or winner_idx is None:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find \'Season\' or \'Winner\' columns. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"Detected season column at index {season_idx}, winner column at index {winner_idx}\\n")\n\n# 7) Extract rows for seasons 1‚Äì44\ndata = []\nfor row in series_table.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]:\n    cells = row.find_all([\'td\',\'th\'])\n    if len(cells) <= max(season_idx, winner_idx):\n        continue\n    # parse season number\n    season_text = cells[season_idx].get_text(strip=True).split()[0]\n    try:\n        season_num = int(season_text)\n    except:\n        continue\n    if season_num < 1 or season_num > 44:\n        continue\n    # parse winner name\n    winner_cell = cells[winner_idx]\n    winner_link = winner_cell.find(\'a\')\n    winner_name = winner_link.get_text(strip=True) if winner_link else winner_cell.get_text(strip=True)\n    data.append({\'season\': season_num, \'winner\': winner_name})\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season_num}: {winner_name}")\n\nif not data:\n    print("‚ö†Ô∏è No winners parsed. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch Survivor Wikipedia page\nurl = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64)\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    print(f"‚Üí HTTP Status: {resp.status_code} OK")\n    print(f"‚Üí Final URL: {resp.url}\\n")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Failed to fetch page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 3) Parse HTML\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Find the correct table: caption "Series overview" or fallback on headers\nwikitables = soup.find_all(\'table\', class_=\'wikitable\')\nprint(f"Found {len(wikitables)} wikitables on the page. Looking for \'Series overview\'...\\n")\nseries_table = None\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, start=1):\n    cap = tbl.find(\'caption\')\n    cap_text = cap.get_text(strip=True).lower() if cap else \'\'\n    print(f"Table {idx}: caption = \'{cap_text}\'")\n    if \'series overview\' in cap_text:\n        series_table = tbl\n        print(f"‚Üí Matched \'Series overview\' table at index {idx}\\n")\n        break\n\nif not series_table:\n    print("No caption match found, trying header‚Äêbased fallback...\\n")\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, start=1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        headers = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'])]\n        print(f"Fallback check Table {idx}: headers = {headers[:7]}")\n        if \'season\' in headers and any(\'winner\' in h for h in headers):\n            series_table = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Fallback matched table at index {idx}\\n")\n            break\n\nif not series_table:\n    print("‚ùå Could not locate the Series overview table.     "role": 'developer',
    "code": 'import os\nimport sys\nimport json\nimport re\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\n\n# 1) Locate the active workspace directory\nworkspace_dirs = [d for d in os.listdir(\'.\') if d.startswith(\'workspace\') and os.path.isdir(d)]\nif not workspace_dirs:\n    print("‚ùå No workspace directory found. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nworkspace_dir = max(workspace_dirs, key=lambda d: os.path.getmtime(d))\nprint(f"Using workspace directory: {workspace_dir}\\n")\n\n# 2) Fetch the Survivor Wikipedia page\nurl = "https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Survivor_(American_TV_series)"\nprint(f"Fetching Survivor page...\\nURL: {url}\\n")\nresp = requests.get(url, headers={\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US\'\n})\ntry:\n    resp.raise_for_status()\n    print(f"‚Üí HTTP Status: {resp.status_code} OK\\n")\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f"‚ùå Failed to fetch page: {e}")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 3) Parse HTML with BeautifulSoup\nsoup = BeautifulSoup(resp.text, \'html.parser\')\n\n# 4) Find the "Series overview" table by caption or fallback on header row containing \'Season\' and \'Winner\'\nwikitables = soup.find_all(\'table\', class_=\'wikitable\')\nprint(f"Found {len(wikitables)} wikitables on the page. Searching for \'Series overview\'...\\n")\nseries_table = None\nfor idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, start=1):\n    cap = tbl.find(\'caption\')\n    cap_text = cap.get_text(strip=True).lower() if cap else \'\'\n    print(f"Table {idx}: caption=\'{cap_text}\'")\n    if \'series overview\' in cap_text:\n        series_table = tbl\n        print(f"‚Üí Matched \'Series overview\' table at index {idx}\\n")\n        break\n\nif not series_table:\n    print("No caption match found, trying header‚Äêbased fallback...\\n")\n    for idx, tbl in enumerate(wikitables, start=1):\n        first_row = tbl.find(\'tr\')\n        if not first_row:\n            continue\n        headers = [th.get_text(strip=True).lower() for th in first_row.find_all([\'th\',\'td\'])]\n        print(f"Fallback check Table {idx}: headers={headers}")\n        if \'season\' in headers and any(\'winner\' in h for h in headers):\n            series_table = tbl\n            print(f"‚Üí Fallback matched table at index {idx}\\n")\n            break\n\nif not series_table:\n    print("‚ùå Could not locate the Series overview table. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\n\n# 5) Determine column indices dynamically\nheader_cells = series_table.find(\'tr\').find_all([\'th\',\'td\'])\ncol_texts = [c.get_text(strip=True) for c in header_cells]\ncol_lower = [t.lower() for t in col_texts]\nprint(f"Series overview columns detected: {col_texts}\\n")\ntry:\n    season_idx = col_lower.index(\'season\')\nexcept ValueError:\n    season_idx = next((i for i,t in enumerate(col_lower) if \'season\' in t), None)\nwinner_idx = next((i for i,t in enumerate(col_lower) if \'winner\' in t), None)\nif season_idx is None or winner_idx is None:\n    print("‚ùå Could not find \'Season\' or \'Winner\' columns. Exiting.")\n    sys.exit(1)\nprint(f"Detected season column at index {season_idx}, winner column at index {winner_idx}\\n")\n\n# 6) Extract season‚Äìwinner pairs with fallback for misaligned cells\ndata = []\nnumeric_pattern = re.compile(r\'^[\\d‚Äì\\-\\s]+$\')\nrows = series_table.find_all(\'tr\')[1:]  # skip header\nfor i, row in enumerate(rows, start=1):\n    cells = row.find_all([\'td\',\'th\'])\n    # Only consider rows with enough cells for season\n    if len(cells) <= season_idx:\n        continue\n    # Parse season number\n    season_text = cells[season_idx].get_text(\' \', strip=True).split()[0]\n    try:\n        season_num = int(season_text)\n    except ValueError:\n        continue\n    if not (1 <= season_num <= 44):\n        continue\n    # Extract primary winner text\n    primary_txt = cells[winner_idx].get_text(\' \', strip=True)\n    # Fallback if primary is blank or numeric (vote count)\n    if not primary_txt or numeric_pattern.fullmatch(primary_txt):\n        # search other cells for name\n        fallback = None\n        for j, cell in enumerate(cells):\n            if j == season_idx:\n                continue\n            link = cell.find(\'a\')\n            candidate = link.get_text(strip=True) if link else cell.get_text(\' \', strip=True)\n            if any(ch.isalpha() for ch in candidate):\n                fallback = candidate\n                print(f"  Season {season_num} fallback: picked cell {j} -> \'{fallback}\' (primary was \'{primary_txt}\')")\n                break\n        winner_name = fallback or primary_txt\n    else:\n        winner_name = primary_txt\n    data.append({\'season\': season_num, \'winner\': winner_name})\n    print(f"Parsed Season {season_num}: {winner_name}")\n\n# 7) Validate and save\nif len(data) != 44:\n    print(f"‚ö†Ô∏è Warning: Parsed {len(data)} seasons (expected 44). Please verify missing entries.")\n# Sort entries by season\ndata_sorted = sorted(data, key=lambda x: x[\'season\'])\nout_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'survivor_winners_list.json\')\nwith open(out_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(data_sorted, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\nprint(f"\\n‚úÖ Successfully wrote {len(data_sorted)} entries to: {out_file}")',
    "description": "Implementation rationale:\n1) Identified the active workspace directory for file output.\n2) Retrieved the Survivor Wikipedia page and confirmed HTTP 200 status.\n3) Parsed the page HTML with BeautifulSoup.\n4) Located the main 'Series overview' wikitable by matching its <caption> text (case-insensitive).
